
#Mages

estate_mages_organization_magisterium = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	#Removed this so AI doesn't sit at negative mages loyalty
	#loyalty = -0.05
	land_share = 5
	influence = 0.2
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { tag = I02 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = sleeper_mages }
		NOT = { has_mages_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	can_select = {
		OR = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = A85
					NOT = { tag = A85 }
				}
				A85 = {	#Magisterium likes you
					has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 200 }
				}
			}
			is_part_of_hre = yes
			tag = A85
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_mages
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				adm_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				adm_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
		has_discovered = 8 #Anbenncost
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = mages_benefits_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_mages_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_magisterium }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_adm_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_adm_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_mages_organization_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_magisterium_relations_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_year = 1445 }
				}
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_mages }
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		global_tax_modifier = 0.05
		imperial_authority = 0.05
	}
	#Removed this so AI doesn't sit at negative mages loyalty
	# conditional_modifier = {
		# trigger = {
			# NOT = { tag = A85 }
			# NOT = {
				# reverse_has_opinion = {
					# who = A85 #Magisterium
					# value = -150
				# }
			# }
		# }
		# modifier = {
			# mages_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
		# }
	# }
	# conditional_modifier = {
		# trigger = {
			# NOT = { tag = A85 }
			# reverse_has_opinion = {
				# who = A85 #Magisterium
				# value = -150
			# }
			# NOT = {
				# reverse_has_opinion = {
					# who = A85 #Magisterium
					# value = -100
				# }
			# }
		# }
		# modifier = {
			# mages_loyalty_modifier = -0.05
		# }
	# }
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = A85 }
			reverse_has_opinion = {
				who = A85 #Magisterium
				value = 100
			}
			NOT = {
				reverse_has_opinion = {
					who = A85 #Magisterium
					value = 150
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			mages_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = A85 }
			reverse_has_opinion = {
				who = A85 #Magisterium
				value = 150
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			mages_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			tag = A85
		}
		modifier = {
			mages_loyalty_modifier = 0.15
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			tag = A85
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_part_of_hre = yes
		}
	}
}

estate_mages_organization_orda_aldresia = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	#Removed this so AI doesn't sit at negative mages loyalty
	loyalty = 0.10
	land_share = 10
	influence = 0.2
	is_valid = {
		tag = A77
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	benefits = {
		innovativeness_gain = 1
		assault_fort_ability = 0.5
		may_recruit_female_generals = yes
	}
}

estate_mages_organization_state = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 10
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { tag = A85 }
		NOT = { tag = I02 }
		NOT = { has_mages_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_mages
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				adm_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				adm_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = mages_benefits_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_mages_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_state }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_adm_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_adm_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_mages_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
				take_estate_land_share_gigantic = { estate = estate_mages }
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.05
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = J33_mage_only_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			mages_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
			mages_influence_modifier = 0.1
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			current_age = age_of_absolutism
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_magisterium
		}
	}
}

	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }

	influence = 0.1

		NOT = { tag = A77 }
	}
	can_select = {

			limit = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_mages
				loyalty = 30
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				adm_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				adm_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = mages_benefits_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_mages_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_guilds }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_adm_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_adm_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_mages_organization_effect = yes
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		#global_tax_modifier = 0.05
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

estate_mages_organization_religious = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	#Removed this so AI doesn't sit at negative mages loyalty
	#loyalty = -0.05
	influence = 0.15
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { tag = A85 }
		NOT = { tag = I02 }
		OR = {
			religion = ravelian
			religion = xhazobkult
			religion = skaldhyrric_faith
			religion = devouring_path
			religion = beast_memory
			religion = rinta_seekers
			religion = sky_domain
			religion = shadow_pact
			religion = rune_scribes
			has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
			has_country_flag = elikhand_magic_khet
			religion = anzalkatsa
		}
		NOT = { has_mages_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_mages
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				adm_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				adm_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = mages_benefits_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_mages_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_religious }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_adm_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_adm_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_mages_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_mages }
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_religious_invalid_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes } }
				set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_state
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		global_missionary_strength = 0.02
		church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		church_influence_modifier = 0.05

		papal_influence = 0.5
		church_power_modifier = 0.5
		monthly_fervor_increase = 1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 40 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 30 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 50 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
	}
}

estate_mages_battlemage_academies = {
	icon = privilege_demand_more_troops
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	land_share = 10
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { tag = I02 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = Y26_maidens_of_mists } # Yinquan MT
		NOT = { has_country_flag = established_zamukaras_flag }
	}
	can_select = {
		army_tradition = 15
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_acolytes
			}
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_acolytes
				influence = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_mages
				influence = 30
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_empowered_mages }
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_army_tradition = -15
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_estate_mages_battlemage_academies
	}
	penalties = {
		army_tradition_decay = 0.01
		country_military_power = -1
	}
	benefits = {
		land_morale = 0.05
	}
	conditional_modifier = {		#part of xia mission tree
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = xia_battlemage_mastery
		}
		modifier = {
			army_tradition_decay = -0.01
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = battlemage_no_decay #Currently Ameion Archeology
		}
		modifier = {
			army_tradition_decay = -0.01
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = no_debuff_battlemages_flg
		}
		modifier = {
			mages_influence_modifier = -0.05
			max_absolutism = 5
			mages_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
			country_military_power = 1
			army_tradition_decay = -0.01
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			personality = ai_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_at_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { army_tradition = 1 }	#if you have hella low army tradition, you're gonna want to turn this off
		}
	}
}

			factor = 1.5
			is_at_war = yes
		}

			factor = 0

		}
	}
}

estate_mages_patronage_of_the_magical_arts = {	#magical patronage
	icon = privilege_give_money
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		prestige = 0.5
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { prestige = 50 }
			add_prestige = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = 0 }
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -25 }
			add_prestige = 20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -50 }
			add_prestige = 25
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 30
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {

				ruler_has_personality = just_personality
				ruler_has_personality = righteous_personality
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_magisterium
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_government_attribute = is_raja
				is_emperor_of_china = yes
			}
		}
	}

estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_damestear
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		NOT = { tag = I02 }
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = damestear
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
			# NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			# NOT = {
				# has_disaster_progress = {
					# disaster = french_revolution
					# value = 1
				# }
			# }
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_mercantilism = 1
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 8
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = damestear
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_DAMESTEAR_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_effect_tooltip
		# hidden_effect = {
		# 	every_owned_province = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			trade_goods = damestear
		# 		}
		# 		add_province_modifier = {
		# 			name = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		# 			duration = -1
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { trade_goods = damestear }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_mages_monopoly_of_damestear_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.12 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { #having the AI use these could lead to an unstoppable downwards spiral if it can't work out how to get rid of them
		factor = 0
	}
}

estate_adventurers_organization_chronicler_grants = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_adventurers_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_adventurers_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_adventurers
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_adventurers
				loyalty = 30
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_adventurers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				mil_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				mil_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
		has_discovered = 8 #Anbenncost
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_adventurers_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_organization_chronicler_grants }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_adventurers
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_mil_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_mil_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_adventurers_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_adventurers_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_adventurers_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_adventurers }
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		mercenary_manpower = -0.2
	}
	benefits = {
		global_institution_spread = 0.2
		innovativeness_gain = 0.25
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_known_country = {
				institution_difference = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 1.4
			num_of_territories = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

					influence = 75
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.9
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
				}
				#The trigger below should make sure that the AI actually keeps this privilege when enacting it early game
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.6
					has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { governing_capacity_percentage = 0.5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 40 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 30 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 50 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_adventurers_ennoblement_of_adventurers }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {

estate_adventurers_cavern_exploration_initiative = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			num_of_colonists = 1
			num_of_colonies = 1
		}
		capital_scope = {
			continent = serpentspine
		}
		NOT = {
			colony = 1
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		global_colonial_growth = 10
		colonist_placement_chance = 0.05
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Domination" }
			enable_estate_action = {
				estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = has_no_effects_on_granted
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Domination" }
			disable_estate_action = {
				estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				disable_estate_action = {
					estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Domination" }
			disable_estate_action = {
				estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				disable_estate_action = {
					estate_action = CAVERN_EXPLORATION_INITIATIVE_ADVENTURERS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			AND = {
				capital_scope = {
					continent = serpentspine
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					has_empty_adjacent_province = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
	}
}

estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_slaves
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = slaves
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = no_longer_monstrous
			tag = R38
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
			# NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			# NOT = {
				# has_disaster_progress = {
					# disaster = french_revolution
					# value = 1
				# }
			# }
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_mercantilism = 1
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 8
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = slaves
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_SLAVES_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves_effect_tooltip

	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { trade_goods = slaves }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_monopoly_of_slaves_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod }
			remove_province_modifier = estate_adventurers_monopoly_of_slaves_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.13 }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

#Monstrous Tribes
estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		governing_capacity = 100
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			num_of_territories = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_territories = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 25 }
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_monstrous_tribes
					influence = 75
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.9
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
				}
				#The trigger below should make sure that the AI actually keeps this privilege when enacting it early game
				AND = {
					governing_capacity_percentage = 0.6
					has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { governing_capacity_percentage = 0.5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 40 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 30 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 50 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_land_rights }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
	}
}

#Church

estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = -0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			tag = Y63 # Anbennar Temporary for Verkal Ozovar, to stop them spreading AW in Haless.
			religion_group = raheni
		}
		NOT = { capital_scope = { superregion = rahen_superregion } }
		any_owned_province = {
			religion_group = halessi
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country }
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
					religion = mystic_accord
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country }
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_effect_tooltip2
		}
		else = { custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_effect_tooltip }
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = rending_started_country } }
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { religion = accretive_path religion = transmutative_path } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
					religion = mystic_accord
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod duration = -1 }
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = {
				any_owned_province = {
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = { # Anbennar
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				tag = Y65	# Arawkelin
				tag = Y69	# Brenulan
				# Sarisung vassals:
				tag = R15	# Nundujisbid
				tag = R37	# Kethur
				tag = R59	# Khappur
				tag = R60	# Sarkhani
			}
		}
	}
}

	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }

estate_burghers_magnate_council = {
	icon = privilege_royal_authority
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		# Dudes who get Magnates
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture_group = alenic
				NOT = {
					primary_culture = wexonard
					primary_culture = marrodic
				}
			}
			culture_group = gerudian
			culture_group = reachman
			primary_culture = city_goblin
			has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_magnate_council # Cannot go invalid by culture shifting
		}
		NOT = { has_disaster = magnate_uprising }
	}
	can_select = {
		#always
	}

estate_daulophs_monopoly_of_metals = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_iron
	max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				trade_goods = iron
				trade_goods = copper
				trade_goods = mithril
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			tooltip = JY_LF_not_trading #Anbennar
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = JY_LF_recent_trade }
			# NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			# NOT = {
				# has_disaster_progress = {
					# disaster = french_revolution
					# value = 1
				# }
			# }
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_mercantilism = 1
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 8
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
					trade_goods = mithril
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_IRON_AND_COPPER_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
					trade_goods = mithril
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_daulophs_monopoly_of_metals_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_daulophs_monopoly_of_metals_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_daulophs_monopoly_of_metals_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_daulophs_monopoly_of_metals_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_daulophs_monopoly_of_metals_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.5 }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

estate_church_sponsored_festivals = {
	icon = privilege_nsc_sponsored_festivals
	loyalty = 0.10
	influence = 0.05

	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_sponsored_festivals_flag
	}

	can_select = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_sponsored_festivals_flag
	}

	on_revoked = { }

	on_granted = { }

	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.10
	}
	benefits = {
		tolerance_own = 1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

estate_mages_empowered_mages = {
	icon = privilege_demand_more_troops
	influence = 0.10
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			religion = bulwari_sun_cult
			has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
		}
		is_chosen_country = yes
		has_country_flag = nsc_banned_artificery
		# so it doesn't appear until you ban artificery
	}
	can_select = { always = no }

	can_revoke = { always = no }

	on_granted = { }

	penalties = {
		army_tradition_decay = 0.01
		country_military_power = -1
	}
	benefits = {
		land_morale = 0.05
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

estate_mages_bardic_general = {
	icon = privilege_demand_more_troops
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_bardic_college
	}
	land_share = 5
	can_select = {
		army_tradition = 5
		estate_influence = {
			estate = estate_mages
			influence = 30
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_army_tradition = -5
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_estate_mages_bardic_general
	}
	penalties = {
		army_tradition_decay = 0.005
	}
	benefits = {
		land_morale = 0.05
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			personality = ai_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_at_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { army_tradition = 1 }	#if you have hella low army tradition, you're gonna want to turn this off
		}
	}
}

#khugdihr
estate_church_khug_ancestral_worshippers = {
	icon = privilege_religious_diplomats
	influence = 0.2
	is_valid = { has_country_flag = ancestral_worshippers_unlocked }
	benefits = { tolerance_heathen = 2 }
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = khug_religion_opinion_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = khug_religious_opinion
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = ancestor_worship
					NOT = {
						has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = khug_religion
						}
					}
				}
				add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = khug_remove_religion_opinion_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = khug_religious_opinion
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = khug_religion
						}
						religion = ancestor_worship
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
				reverse_remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = khug_religion
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

estate_mages_supply_more_iron = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_iron
	influence = 0.2
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = { tag = I02 }
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = iron
			NOT = { province_id = 4208 }
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals }
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_supply_more_iron_effect
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = iron
				NOT = { province_id = 4208 }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = krak_supply_more_iron duration = 3650 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = krak_supply_more_iron
			}
			remove_province_modifier = krak_supply_more_iron
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_supply_more_iron_revoke
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = krak_supply_more_iron }
			remove_province_modifier = krak_supply_more_iron
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_supply_more_iron_revoke
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = krak_supply_more_iron }
			remove_province_modifier = krak_supply_more_iron
		}
	}
	penalties = {}
	benefits = {}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = { country_event = { id = flavor_krak.107 } }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}

estate_mages_perform_icecraft = {
	icon = privilege_tolerance_heathen
	can_select = {
		always = no
	}
	is_valid = {
		tag = I02
		has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_perform_icecraft
		NOT = { has_country_flag = revoke_mage_estate_spells }
	}
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		set_country_flag = revoke_mage_estate_spells # on_invalid gives a notification, on_revoked does not.
	}
	on_invalid = {
		clr_country_flag = revoke_mage_estate_spells
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

xhazobkult_flesh_of_flesh = {
	icon = privilege_seek_support_of_clergy
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion = xhazobkult
		has_ruler_flag = undergoing_xhazob_ritual
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = xhazobkult_attempting_xhaz
			has_ruler_flag = undergoing_xhazob_ritual
		}
		OR = {
			government = tribal
			government = monarchy
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_heir = yes }
			kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	penalties = {
		heir_chance = -1
		stability_cost_modifier = 0.75
	}
	benefits = {
		yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.01
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
}

estate_mages_sun_elf_evocation = {
	icon = privilege_seek_support_of_clergy
	max_absolutism = 0
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { AND = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes OR = { has_country_flag = nsc_privilege_burgher_influence has_country_flag = nsc_privilege_noble_influence } } } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = bulwari
			has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
		}
		has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_evocation
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		shock_damage = 0.10
		defensiveness = 0.05
	}
	conditional_modifier = {        #Burghers
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = nsc_privilege_burgher_influence
        }
        modifier = {
            max_absolutism = -5
            burghers_influence_modifier = 0.1
            mages_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
        }
    }
    conditional_modifier = {        #Nobility
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = nsc_privilege_noble_influence
        }
        modifier = {
            max_absolutism = -5
            nobles_influence_modifier = 0.1
            mages_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
        }
    }
    conditional_modifier = {        #Mages
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = nsc_privilege_magi_influence
        }
        modifier = {
			mages_influence_modifier = 0.1
            mages_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
        }
    }
	conditional_modifier = {        #Both
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = nsc_privilege_both_influence
        }
        modifier = {
            nobles_influence_modifier = 0.05
			burghers_influence_modifier = 0.05
            mages_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
        }
    }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
}

estate_church_protected_burials = {
	icon = privilege_build_jain_temple
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
	}
	penalties = {
		global_manpower_modifier = -0.10
	}
	benefits = {
		prestige = 0.5
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = reduced_aw_ghouls_tt
		if = {
			limit = { prestige = 50 }
			add_prestige = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = 0 }
			add_prestige = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -25 }
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -50 }
			add_prestige = 20
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 25
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = reduced_aw_ghouls_tt
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

#Beikdugang Flamekeepers
estate_mages_flamekeepers = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			mission_completed = Y15_northeast_passage
			overlord = { mission_completed = Y15_northeast_passage }
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		OR = {
			mission_completed = Y15_the_flamekeepers
			overlord = { mission_completed = Y15_the_flamekeepers }
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = Y15_flamekeeper_granted
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_climate = arctic }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic }
			remove_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		add_stability = -1
		custom_tooltip = Y15_flamekeeper_revoked
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic }
			remove_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = Y15_flamekeeper_revoked
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic }
			remove_province_modifier = Y15_flamekeeper_arctic
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.15
	}
	benefits = {
		naval_attrition = -0.2
		trade_range_modifier = 0.25
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = 50 }
			estate_influence = { estate = estate_mages influence = 40 }
		}
		modifier = {
			naval_attrition = -0.2
			trade_range_modifier = 0.25
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
}

		 			trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
		 		}
		 		add_province_modifier = {
		 			name = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		 			duration = -1
		 		}
		 	}
		 }
	}

	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = copper
					trade_goods = iron
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_balgarsmiths_mining_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_balgarsmiths_mining_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Z36_balgarsmiths_production_bonus
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

#Barumand
estate_nobility_permanent_embassies = {
    icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
    max_absolutism = -10
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
    loyalty = 0.20
    influence = 0.10
    is_valid = {
        has_country_flag = barumand_embassy_privilege
    }
    can_revoke = {
        always = yes
    }

    on_granted = {
        custom_tooltip = barumand_increase_subject_opinion_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_subject_country = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        has_opinion_modifier = {
                            who = ROOT
                            modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                        }
                    }
                }
                add_opinion = {
                    who = ROOT
                    modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                }
            }
        }
    }
	on_revoked = {
        custom_tooltip = barumand_remove_increase_subject_opinion_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_subject_country = {
                limit = {
                    has_opinion_modifier = {
                        who = ROOT
                        modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                    }
                }
                remove_opinion = {
                    who = ROOT
                    modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                }
            }
        }
    }

    on_invalid = {
        custom_tooltip = barumand_remove_increase_subject_opinion_tt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_subject_country = {
                limit = {
                    has_opinion_modifier = {
                        who = ROOT
                        modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                    }
                }
                remove_opinion = {
                    who = ROOT
                    modifier = barumand_increase_subject_opinion
                }
            }
        }
    }

    benefits = {
        improve_relation_modifier = 0.1
    }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
}

	}

		hidden_effect = {

					superregion = east_serpentspine_superregion
				}

					name = estate_burghers_improved_supply_routes_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}

			}
		}
	}

	}

			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				has_terrain = cavern

			}
		}
	}

estate_burghers_rudmen_traders = {
	icon = privilege_new_world_mission
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		tag = H51
		has_country_flag = freemarches_rudmen_traders_unlocked 
		
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = fur
		}
	}

	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_rudmen_traders_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			add_mercantilism = -2
	 	}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = fur
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_rudmen_traders_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_rudmen_traders_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H51_rudmen_traders_production_bonus
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
}

		}

		}

			vazhatun_decrease_observation_efficiency_large = yes
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		if = {
			limit = { mission_completed = vazhatun_experts_of_magic }
			vazhatun_decrease_observation_efficiency_massive = yes

		}

	penalties = {

	}

#Eduz-Vacyn

estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute = {
	icon = privilege_promote_maratha_nobility
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
         		religion_group = bulwari
         		has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
        	}
		NOT = { has_mages_special_organization_privilege = yes }
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes }
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_mages
				loyalty = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				adm_power = 100
				stability = 1
			}
			else = {
				adm_power = 200
				stability = 2
			}
		}
	}
	can_revoke = {
		always = no
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = mages_benefits_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_mages_organization_privilege = yes
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_mages
						loyalty = 60
					}
				}
				add_adm_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
				add_adm_power = -200
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_cost_tooltip
			custom_tooltip = estate_mages_organization_revoke_tooltip
			clear_mages_organization_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
				take_estate_land_share_massive = { estate = estate_mages }
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_mages_jaherian_invalid_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_mages_organization_privilege = yes } }
				set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_state
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		global_unrest = -1
		global_missionary_strength = 0.02
		church_influence_modifier = 0.1
		church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		monthly_fervor_increase = 1
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = vacyntassy_jaherian_statute_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			diplomatic_reputation = 1
			all_estate_loyalty_equilibrium = 0.05
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 40 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 30 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 50 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_absolutism_active = yes
		}
	}
}

	on_invalid_province = {

			value = 0
		}
	}

		tag = I16
		mission_completed = gor_burad_steam_baron_ascendancy
	}

	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_steam_barons_independent_governance_granted_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_terrain = cavern
				region = serpentreach_region
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_steam_baron_independent_governance_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_steam_barons_independent_governance_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_steam_baron_independent_governance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_steam_baron_independent_governance_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_steam_barons_independent_governance_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_steam_baron_independent_governance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_steam_baron_independent_governance_mod
		}
	}

		factor = 0
	}

	influence = 0.05

			religion_group = bulwari

				}
			}

			tag = F99
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_dictate_understanding_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = bulwari }
				NOT = { superregion = bulwar_superregion }
				NOT = { #Evil Religions
					religion = xhazobkult
					religion = devouring_path

					religion = chahinanito
					religion = song_servants
					religion = leechfather
				}
				NOT = {
					culture = sun_elf
					culture = desert_elf
					culture = dawn_elf
					culture = zanlibi
					culture_group = bulwari
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_church_dictate_understanding_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {

	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_dictate_understanding_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_dictate_understanding_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_dictate_understanding_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_dictate_understanding_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_dictate_understanding_mod
		}

estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_slaves
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	loyalty = 0.15
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = G53_independent_trading_unlocked_flag
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = slaves
		}
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				slaves = 1
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = empkeios_events.1200
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = empkeios_slaveIncome_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = empkeios_events.2603
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = slaves
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_empkeios_independent_trading_revoke_tt
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_empkeios_independent_trading_revoke_tt
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_slaver_independent_trading_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

	cooldown_years = 10 
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = buffed_monopolies
		}
		modifier = {
			burghers_privilege_slots = 1
		}
	}
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = empkeios_events.2602 }
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = { has_country_flag = unlocked_estate_burghers_multiracial_crop_rotation }

	can_revoke = {  always = yes }

	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_multiracial_crop_rotation_tooltip
	}

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { trade_goods = serpentbloom trade_goods = fungi } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = skewered_drake_crop_caves duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { trade_goods = grain trade_goods = livestock } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = skewered_drake_crop_other duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
	}

	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = skewered_drake_crop_caves
		remove_province_modifier = skewered_drake_crop_other
	}

	benefits = {
		global_unrest = -1
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

estate_church_sand_molding = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost_desert
	max_absolutism = -10
	land_share = 5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	influence = 0.10
	loyalty = 0.10
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_church_sand_molding }
	}
	can_select = {
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_terrain = desert
				has_terrain = coastal_desert
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_2
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_gt_2
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_1
				}
				custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_gt_1
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_gt
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_2
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = coastal_desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_coastal_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}	
			}	
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_1
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = coastal_desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_coastal_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}	
			}	
			else = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_terrain = coastal_desert
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_coastal_desert
						duration = -1
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_2
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_rt_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sand_molding_1
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_rt_1
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sand_molding_rt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_coastal_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_coastal_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_desert
						has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_coastal_desert
					}
				}
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_little_coastal_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_big_coastal_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_desert
				remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sand_molding_super_coastal_desert
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

estate_church_sandstorm_summoning = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost_desert
	influence = 0.10
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning }
	}
	can_select = {  }
	benefits = {
		church_privilege_slots = 1
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sandstorm_summoning
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning_buff_gt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning_gt
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					owner = { has_country_flag = irkorzik_upgraded_sandstorm_summoning }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall_buff }
					has_building = mage_tower
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_building = mage_tower
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_wall_buff }
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff }
			remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_sandstorm_summoning_buff
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_sandstorm_summoning_buff_rt
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

#Exwes
estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier = {
	icon = privilege_ducats
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = 0
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 2 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier }
		has_estate = estate_burghers
	}
	can_select = {
		has_estate = estate_burghers
	}
	can_revoke = {
		estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			higher_than_influence = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier_effect_tt
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_wharf_trade_goods = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = impressment_offices
						has_building = wharf
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
			}
			remove_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier_revoke_effect_tt
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			loyalty = -20
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
			}
			remove_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exwes_leading_naval_supplier_revoke_effect_tt
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
			}
			remove_province_modifier = burghers_estate_exwes_wharf_trade_up
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				AND = {
					has_wharf_trade_goods = yes
					OR = {
						has_building = wharf
						has_building = impressment_offices
					}
				}
				value = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_vb_riverblade = {
	icon = privilege_spawn_rajput_regiments

	loyalty = -0.05
	influence = 0.05
	land_share = 5
	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }

	can_select = {
		has_country_flag = G84_panykorun
	}

	can_revoke = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	is_valid = {
		has_country_flag = G84_panykorun
	}

	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = G84_panykorun_privileges_upgraded } }
			custom_tooltip = G84_panykorun_privilege_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = G84_panykorun_privilege_upgraded_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { primary_culture = sarda }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = G84_riverblade_attaches
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = G84_panykorun_privileges_upgraded }
				every_subject_country = {
					limit = { OR = { primary_culture = dolindhan primary_culture = rzentur } }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = G84_riverblade_attaches
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_revoked = {
		every_subject_country = {
			remove_country_modifier = G84_riverblade_attaches
		}
	}

	benefits = {
		reduced_liberty_desire = 5
		discipline = 0.05
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

estate_church_spring_tolerance = {

	max_absolutism = -5
	conditional_modifier = { trigger = { has_absolutism_reduction_for_estate_privileges = yes } modifier = { max_absolutism = 1 } }
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = -0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion = spring_court
	}
	can_select = {
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
			value = 4
			OR = {
				religion = summer_court
				religion = autumn_court
				religion = winter_court
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_spring_tolerance_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = summer_court
					religion = autumn_court
					religion = winter_court
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
		}	
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_spring_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_spring_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_spring_tolerance_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

	influence_scaled_conditional_modifier = {	#Modifier that are applied if the specified conditions are true. At 100% Influence you gain 100% of the modifier.
		modifier = { same_religion_advisor_cost = -0.2 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}

estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_cloth
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			has_country_flag = buffed_monopolies
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = tropical_wood
		}
		has_country_flag = karakhanbar_monopoly_on_fuel
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tropical_wood = 1
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = karakhanbar_upgrade_of_monopoly
			}
			add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
				years = 12
				trigger = {
					trade_goods = tropical_wood
				}
				custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_TROPICAL_WOOD_DESC
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
				years = 8
				trigger = {
					trade_goods = tropical_wood
				}
				custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_TROPICAL_WOOD_DESC
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_effect_tooltip
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = tropical_wood
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_noble_monopoly_of_fuel_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		monthly_karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_power = 0.5
	}
	cooldown_years = 10
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.20 }
	}
	ai_will_do = { #having the AI use these could lead to an unstoppable downwards spiral if it can't work out how to get rid of them
		factor = 0
	}
}
